I have lived in Sunshine for nearly twenty years, and except for special circumstances in the past few years, basically every year I am going to Yalong Bay to stay for a few days and then come here again. On this trip, we also visited the Sheraton Mangrove Forest first, and the last stop was Sunshine. I was given a surprise when I came here! It is actually being renovated again. It has been renovated for two or three consecutive years. In the past, the renovation did not affect rest, but this time it is different! I started chipping away at the wall at a little after 8 o'clock in the morning. I called the front desk and didn't stop until after 8:30. I basically didn't want to sleep anymore. Then there is no refrigerator or iron in the room of the five-star hotel. I called the waiter to bring one. The waiter threw the refrigerator on the table and left. I originally wanted to make do with it, but the noise was too much. If you can put it into the cabinet with difficulty, you will know this by watching the video below. The hotel's swimming pool was surrounded by a cordon all day on the first day, and the staff were cleaning the pool. They cleaned it all morning the next day. When I asked at the front desk, I was told that you can swim after 2 p.m., and you can also swim yesterday. . What‚Äôs funny is that you can swim, why do you have to surround the cordon? The weirdest thing is the afternoon tea that comes with the package. The electronic screen in the lobby shows that it is until 6:30 p.m., but when I asked the staff in the lobby at 4:59, I was told that it can only be until 5 o'clock, and it is no longer available! In fact, it doesn't matter whether you want to have this afternoon tea or not, but having a five-star hotel with such a service attitude and racing against time to give you points is really annoying! Fortunately, the hotel manager appeared in time and handled it properly, resolving this conflict that should not have happened. It can only be said that Sunshine‚Äôs senior management still has a deep understanding of service, which is worthy of recognition! The newly renovated room has no smell. The type-c interface on the wall is very convenient. The black one is simple and elegant. It realizes intelligent control of most of the equipment in the room. It is finally considered to be advancing with the times. It's a pity that the pool bar has not been able to restore its previous self-service barbecue and resident Filipino singers, but the affordable a la carte prices and the chef's exquisite craftsmanship can be regarded as a small bright spot in a place like Sanya Bay. The above advantages are also the reasons why I can give it a neutral rating this time. Finally, I would like to say that I still feel a little sad when I see the deserted lobby of Sunshine. I hope Sunshine can regain its original shadow and restore its former glory through this renovation, both in terms of hardware and software.

You can choose here for your first impression when you first arrive in Sanya and the perfect ending when you leave Sanya. It is very close to the seaside and beach. It is separated by a road, so it is convenient to take a taxi or bus. You don't have to worry about going to the airport, shopping at Sanya duty-free stores, or visiting scenic spots. It can be said that it is the C position of Sanya Bay, a very good location.
The service is very good. If you are serious about traveling to Sanya, you should choose a star-rated hotel. As soon as the car arrives at the lobby, the concierge will come to pick up your luggage. After checking in, you will be sent back to the room. The concierge Li Ning will introduce the hotel and Sanya along the way. He is very professional but It's not overly professional, comfortable and down-to-earth. It makes people feel like they're back at home. They won't feel unfamiliar with Sanya and the hotel at all. The service is really good and comes from the heart. Thank you Manager Lu and concierge Xiao Li, because their sincere and enthusiastic service helped the hotel avoid problems. Despite some shortcomings, I will still choose Sunshine when I come to Sanya in the future and when my friends come to Sanya! ! !
Hotel facilities - everything that a star-rated hotel should have, such as swimming pools and gyms, there is nowhere to go even if you don't leave the hotel. The room - spacious and comfortable, large space, hygienic and clean, stable water pressure and temperature, and powerful air conditioning. Although it is close to the seaside, it will not be very humid if the doors and windows are closed and the air conditioning is turned on.
Restaurant - The only thing I didn't experience this time was the hotel's restaurant. When I made the reservation, I didn't order breakfast because I wanted to sleep until I woke up naturally. I will definitely make it up next time and enjoy it!
